PROHIBITION ON TAXATION OF UNITED STATES 
1
ASSISTANCE 
2
SEC. 7013. (a) PROHIBITION ON TAXATION.—None 
3
of the funds appropriated under titles III through VI of 
4
this Act may be made available to provide assistance for 
5
a foreign country under a new bilateral agreement gov-
6
erning the terms and conditions under which such assist-
7

9

10
the foreign government, and the Secretary of State shall 
11

12
lateral agreements, as necessary, to conform with this re-
13
quirement. 
14
(b) NOTIFICATION AND REIMBURSEMENT OF FOR-
15

16
the total taxes assessed during fiscal year 2026 on funds 
17
appropriated by this Act and prior Acts making appropria-
18
tions for the Department of State, foreign operations, and 
19
related programs by a foreign government or entity 
20
against United States assistance programs, either directly 
21
or through grantees, contractors, and subcontractors, shall 
22
be withheld from obligation from funds appropriated for 
23
assistance for fiscal year 2027 and for prior fiscal years 
24
and allocated for the central government of such country 
25

267
•HR 7006 EH
or for the West Bank and Gaza program, as applicable, 
1
if, not later than September 30, 2027, such taxes have 
2
not been reimbursed. 
3
(c) DE MINIMIS EXCEPTION.—Foreign taxes of a de 
4
minimis nature shall not be subject to the provisions of 
5
subsection (b). 
6
(d) REPROGRAMMING OF FUNDS.—Funds withheld 
7

8

9
ance for countries which do not assess taxes on United 
10
States assistance or which have an effective arrangement 
11

12
and that can reasonably accommodate such assistance in 
13
